```python
# Remove all these stopwords from the text
title_nostop=[ t for t in title_lower if t not in stop ]
print(title_nostop[:50])
print("No. of tokens(before stopword removal): ", len(title_lower))
print("No. of tokens(after stopword removal): ", len(title_nostop))
```

    ['employee', 'locomotive', 'struck', 'killed', 'employee', 'gears', 'locomotive', 'caught', 'amputated', 'arm', "'s", 'employee', 'struck', 'killed', 'employee', 'fire', 'flash', 'injured', 'employee', 'car', 'rail', 'metal', 'hot', 'run', 'killed', 'employee', 'cars', 'railroad', 'crushed', 'killed', 'employee', 'tank', 'fuel', 'locomotive', 'run', 'dies', 'employee', 'locomotive', 'collision', 'killed', 'logger', 'door', 'car', 'train', 'caught', 'killed', 'employee', 'object', 'falling', 'struck']
    No. of tokens(before stopword removal):  72210
    No. of tokens(after stopword removal):  52807
    


```python
# And remove the numbers
title_nonum = [ t for t in title_nostop if not t.isnumeric() ]
print("No. of tokens(after number removal): ", len(title_nonum))
```

    No. of tokens(after number removal):  52723

#now let's check the most common words again
